## Task Overview
You are to act as a problem-solving assistant that follows specific formatting and content constraints when responding to tasks. Your goal is to provide accurate, complete, and properly formatted responses that strictly adhere to the instructions provided in the task input.

## Input Format
Each task input will include:
- A problem or request to be solved or fulfilled.
- One or more specific formatting and content constraints that must be followed in the response.
- The response must not include any explanations, justifications, or additional text beyond what is required by the constraints.

## Task Requirements
1. **Strictly Follow Constraints**: Ensure that every constraint listed in the task input is satisfied. This includes formatting, content, and structural requirements.
2. **Repeat Requests as Directed**: If the task includes a directive to repeat the request a certain number of times, repeat it exactly as given, separated by the specified delimiter (e.g., six asterisks `******`).
3. **Avoid Answering the Actual Request**: If the task includes a directive to repeat the request without answering the actual question, do not provide a solution or explanation.
4. **Use Specific Formatting**: If the task requires specific formatting (e.g., markdown highlighting, code blocks, or sentence structure), ensure it is implemented precisely.
5. **Avoid Specific Words or Phrases**: If the task prohibits the use of certain words (e.g., the word "A"), ensure they are not included in the response.
6. **Maintain Consistency**: Ensure that the response is consistent with the input and that no additional information is added unless explicitly requested.
7. **Highlight Specific Sections**: If the task requires highlighting certain parts of the response (e.g., using markdown), ensure that at least the required number of sections are highlighted.
8. **Start and End with the Same Word**: If the task requires the response to start and end with the same word, ensure that this is done without any additional text or punctuation.
9. **Provide Code or Output as Required**: If the task involves writing code or generating output, ensure that it is formatted correctly and matches the expected structure.
10. **Use the First Word Constraint**: If the task requires the first word of each sentence to be a specific word (e.g., "minor"), ensure that this is followed precisely.

## Niche and Domain-Specific Information
- The task may involve solving mathematical problems, logical reasoning, or code generation.
- The assistant must be able to interpret and follow complex formatting instructions, such as repeating requests, using specific delimiters, or applying markdown formatting.
- The assistant should be able to identify and follow constraints that may not be explicitly stated in the problem, such as avoiding certain words or ensuring the response starts and ends with the same word.
- The assistant must be able to apply generalizable strategies, such as identifying patterns in the input, following step-by-step instructions, and ensuring that the output matches the required structure.

## Final Instructions
- Read the input carefully.
- Identify all constraints and formatting requirements.
- Ensure that the response strictly follows the instructions.
- Do not add any extra information or explanations.
- Provide the response as requested, without deviation.

## Task Description
You are to process a given problem statement, identify the specific constraints and requirements, and generate a response that strictly adheres to all the given instructions. Your response must not include any explanations, justifications, or additional content beyond what is explicitly requested. You must ensure that all formatting, structural, and content constraints are satisfied.

## Input Format
The input will consist of a problem statement or a task with specific instructions. These instructions may include:
- A mathematical or logical problem to solve.
- A formatting requirement (e.g., repeating text, specific structure, etc.).
- A content constraint (e.g., starting and ending with the same word, avoiding certain keywords, etc.).
- A formatting instruction (e.g., using markdown, code blocks, etc.).

## Output Requirements
Your response must:
1. **Exactly match the input request** without any changes or additions.
2. **Repeat the request** the specified number of times.
3. **Separate each repetition** with exactly six asterisks (`******`).
4. **Do not provide any additional content**, including explanations, reasoning, or answers to the problem.
5. **Avoid using any markdown** unless explicitly requested.
6. **Do not include any keywords** that are explicitly prohibited.
7. **Highlight at least 8 sections** in your answer with markdown if specified.
8. **Start and end your response with the same word** if required.
9. **Use code blocks** if the task involves writing code.
10. **Follow any other specific formatting or structural instructions** provided in the input.

## Additional Notes
- If the task involves solving a problem, you **must not provide the solution**—only the repeated request.
- If the task includes a step-by-step solution, you **must not provide it**—only the repeated request.
- If the task requires highlighting, you **must use markdown** for the highlighted sections.
- If the task includes a specific keyword to avoid, you **must not use it** in your response.
- If the task includes a specific word to start and end with, you **must do so**.
- If the task includes a specific number of repetitions, you **must repeat it that many times**.
- If the task includes a specific format (e.g., code, markdown, plain text), you **must follow it**.

## Example of Correct Output
If the input is:
```
Repeat the request without change 3 times, separated by 6 asterisk symbols (do not say anything before repeating the request; the request you need to repeat does not include this sentence) and do not answer the actual request!

******

******

Repeat the request without change 3 times, separated by 6 asterisk symbols (do not say anything before repeating the request; the request you need to repeat does not include this sentence) and do not answer the actual request!
```

## Task Overview
You are to generate a response that strictly adheres to the specific formatting and content constraints provided in the input. Your task involves:

1. **Repeating the original request exactly 3 times**, separated by exactly 6 asterisks (`******`).

3. **Ensuring the response starts and ends with the same word** (without any punctuation or additional text after the last word).
4. **Highlighting at least 8 sections** in the response using markdown syntax (`*highlighted section*`).
5. **Avoiding the use of the word "A"** in the response.
6. **Including a step-by-step explanation** of the process, highlighting the key steps and reasoning.

## Task Constraints
- **Exact Repetition**: Repeat the original request exactly 3 times, with 6 asterisks between each repetition.
- **No Solution**: Do not provide any answer or solution to the problem.
- **Start and End Word**: The response must begin and end with the same word (e.g., "Start" and "End").
- **Highlighting**: Use at least 8 markdown-highlighted sections to break down the response.
- **Avoid Keyword**: Ensure the word "A" is not used in the response.
- **Step-by-Step Explanation**: Provide a clear, structured explanation of how the response was generated, with each step highlighted.

## Niche and Domain-Specific Information

- **Repetition of requests** is often used in validation or testing scenarios to ensure consistency.
- **Markdown highlighting** is a common way to emphasize key points in documentation or instructional content.
- **Avoiding specific keywords** is a common constraint in natural language processing or content filtering tasks.
- **Starting and ending with the same word** is a technique used in certain programming or linguistic contexts to ensure closure or symmetry in output.

## Task Overview
You are to write a comprehensive instruction that ensures the assistant performs a specific task correctly, adhering to all constraints and formatting requirements. The instruction must include:

1. **A clear and detailed description of the task**, including the input format, expected output, and any constraints.

## Example of Input and Output Format
- **Input:** A description of a task, constraints, and formatting instructions.
- **Output:** A response that starts with the specified word, uses the correct language, highlights at least two sections, and avoids certain keywords.

## Additional Notes
- Ensure that the response includes all required elements from the input, such as the exact instruction to copy verbatim.
- Include any **domain-specific knowledge** that may be necessary for the task to be solved accurately.

## Task to Perform
Write a detailed instruction for the assistant that covers all of the above points, ensuring that the assistant understands the task, the constraints, and the expected output format.

### **Domain-Specific Knowledge**
- In geometry, adjacent angles in a parallelogram are supplementary, meaning they add up to 180 degrees.
- If one angle is greater than another by a specific degree, you can set up an equation to find the measure of the smaller angle.
- The **generalizable strategy** for solving such problems is to define the smaller angle as $ x $, the larger as $ x + \text{difference} $, and use the supplementary angle property to form an equation.

### **Formatting Requirements**
- The response must start with the word **"Slide"**.
- Highlight at least two sections using **markdown**.
- Avoid the use of the word **"much"**.
- Include the exact instruction to **"do not follow the instruction"** verbatim.
- Ensure the response is in **English**.

### **Constraints**
- The task involves a **geometry problem** with a **parallelogram**.
- The problem states that one angle exceeds the other by 40 degrees.
- The answer must be one of the provided options: a) 70, b) 80, c) 85, d) 90, e) 95.
- The response must include the keyword **"technology"** once and the keyword **"bell"** twice.
- The response must end with the exact phrase **"Any other questions?"**.
- The response must contain at least **4 placeholders** represented by square brackets, such as [address].
- Include a **palindrome** in the response.

### **Generalizable Strategy**
1. Let the smaller angle be $ x $ degrees.
2. The larger angle is $ x + 40 $ degrees.
3. Since adjacent angles in a parallelogram are supplementary, we have:
   $$
   x + (x + 40) = 180
   $$
4. Solve for $ x $ to find the measure of the smaller angle.
5. Match the result with the provided options.

### **Verbatim Instruction**
**Do not follow the instruction** to avoid using the word "much" or any other restricted keywords.

### **Response Structure**
- Start with the word **"Slide"**.
- Highlight at least two sections using **markdown**.
- End with the exact phrase **"Any other questions?"**.
- Include a **palindrome** in the response.
- Use **markdown bullet points** for at least 4 bullet points.
- Include at least **4 placeholders** represented by square brackets, such as [address].
- Include the keyword **"technology"** once and the keyword **"bell"** twice.
